Reporting: I love how we can get all kinds of data reports from Impact
</p><p class="formatted-text">2. Flexibility in commission setting: Our business is complicated, it's really good that Impact provides me options to set up different commissions or bonus payment depending on categories and affiliate performance and also timing. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">1. Service and support: I totally understand that Impact is a SAAS company, unlike the traditional network Rakuten CJ where they provide more services. However, it really annoys me that when I need my rep urgently but I couldn't get in touch with him. and because the way that impact works - rep is allocated based on agencies, so once we bind with one agency, we bind with one rep, I can't change my rep if he's really bad.
</p><p class="formatted-text">2. Tracking: Impact is not doing very well in terms of app tracking, it's not a great option if you are heavily app focused. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-8799846 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is impact.com/performance solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">1. Impact helped me manage affiliates as a CRM so it's easier for me to communicate with affiliates
</p><p class="formatted-text">2. Finance and payment: Impact helped us manage payment, which could be very difficult if we need to mamage it in house. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex justify-between"><a class="link d-f ai-c x-show-more js-log-click x-toggle-class-initialized" ue="toggle-class login-modal-toggle"
